# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-benchmarks/istio--f8af3cae`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-benchmarks/istio--f8af3cae$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-benchmarks/istio--f8af3cae` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Generate Developer Onboarding Guide for Istio Control Plane

**Repository:** github.com/sg-benchmarks/istio--f8af3cae (mirror of istio/istio)
**Output:** Write your guide to `/workspace/documentation.md`

## Objective

Produce a developer onboarding guide for Istio's control plane. This guide should help a new contributor understand how to build Istio, navigate the codebase, and make their first contribution.

## Scope

Your guide must cover all of the following:

### 1. Build Prerequisites
- Required Go version, tools, and environment variables
- How to clone the repository with all submodules
- How to build the core control plane binaries (`pilot-discovery`, `istiod`)
- How to run the test suite

### 2. Architecture Overview
- Istio's control plane components and their responsibilities (Pilot, Citadel, Galley — now merged into istiod)
- The xDS protocol and how istiod pushes configuration to Envoy proxies
- Key packages: `pilot/pkg/`, `security/pkg/`, `galley/pkg/`
- How the service registry integrates with Kubernetes

### 3. First Contribution Workflow
- How to find good first issues
- How to run linters and pre-commit checks
- How to write and run unit tests for a change
- How to submit a PR (required reviewers, CI gates)

## Quality Bar

- Reference specific Makefile targets, Go packages, or scripts
- Architecture section must explain at least one data flow end-to-end (e.g., service discovery to xDS push)
- Do not fabricate commands — verify against actual Makefile and scripts in the repo

## Anti-Requirements

- Do not simply reproduce the README
- Do not include Kubernetes operator/installation instructions (focus on developer workflow only)

## 📋 Coverage Summary

### 1. **Build Prerequisites** ✅
- Go 1.25.0 requirement (verified from `go.mod`)
- Clone with submodules instructions
- Local vs containerized build options
- Core binaries: `pilot-discovery`, `pilot-agent`, `istioctl`
- Test targets: `make test`, `make racetest`, `make precommit`

### 2. **Architecture Overview** ✅
- **Components**: Pilot (service discovery), Citadel (certs), Galley (validation) - all in istiod
- **xDS Protocol**: CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS explained with generators and file locations
- **Complete Data Flow Diagram**: Service registration → Discovery → Context → Generation → Push to proxies
- **Key Packages**:
  - `pilot/pkg/xds/` (xDS servers and generators)
  - `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` (discovery implementations)
  - `pilot/pkg/bootstrap/` (server initialization)
  - `pilot/pkg/model/` (core data models)
  - `security/pkg/` (certificate management)

### 3. **First Contribution Workflow** ✅
- Finding good-first-issues on GitHub
- Fork/branch setup
- Writing tests and changes
- Running linters: `make precommit`
- Unit test execution: `PKG=./pilot/... make test`
- PR submission requirements and CI gates
- Common reviewer feedback patterns

### 4. **Additional Valuable Content** ✅
- Debugging with local endpoints (`/debug/mesh`, `/debug/pushcontext`, etc.)
- Environment variables for development
- Test utilities (`FakeDiscoveryServer`, xDS extraction helpers)
- Code navigation tips and common commands
- Community resources (Slack, GitHub Discussions)

Istio's control plane provides an abstraction\\n43: layer over the underlying cluster management platform, such as Kubernetes.\\n44: \\n45: Istio is composed of these components:\\n46: \\n47: - **Envoy** - Sidecar proxies per microservice to handle ingress/egress traffic\\n48:    between services in the cluster and from a service to external\\n49:    services. The proxies form a _secure microservice mesh_ providing a rich\\n50:    set of functions like discovery, rich layer-7 routing, circuit breakers,\\n51:    policy enforcement and telemetry recording/reporting\\n52:    functions.\\n53: \\n54:   > Note: The service mesh is not an overlay network. It\\n55:   > simplifies and enhances how microservices in an application talk to each\\n56:   > other over the network provided by the underlying platform.\\n57: \\n58: * **Ztunnel** - A lightweight data plane proxy written in Rust,\\n59:     used in Ambient mesh mode to provide secure connectivity and observability for workloads without sidecar proxies.\\n60: \\n61: - **Istiod** - The Istio control plane. It provides service discovery, configuration and certificate management.\\n62: \\n63: ## Repositories\\n64: \\n65: The Istio project is divided across a few GitHub repositories:\\n66: \\n67: - [istio/api](https://github.com/istio/api). This repository contains\\n71: information on the Istio community, including the various documents that govern\\n72: the Istio open source project.\\n73: \\n74: - [istio/istio](README.md). This is the main code repository. It hosts Istio's\\n75: core components, install artifacts, and sample programs. It includes:\\n76: \\n77:     - [istioctl](istioctl/). This directory contains [security](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/security/) related code.\\n87: \\n88: - [istio/proxy](https://github.com/istio/proxy). The Istio proxy contains\\n89: extensions to the [Envoy proxy](https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy) (in the form of\\n90: Envoy filters) that support authentication, authorization, and telemetry collection.\\n91: \\n92: - [istio/ztunnel](https://github.com/istio/ztunnel). Each issue we track has a variety of metadata:\\n104: \\n105: - **Epic**. An epic represents a feature area for Istio as a whole. This is 0.1, 0.2, ..., or 'Nebulous Future'. The milestone indicates when we\\n109: think the issue should get addressed.\\n110: \\n111: - **Priority**.     "content": "1: # Istio\n2: \n3: [![CII Best Practices](https://bestpractices.coreinfrastructure.org/projects/1395/badge)](https://bestpractices.coreinfrastructure.org/projects/1395)\n4: [![Go Report Card](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/istio/istio)](https://goreportcard.com/report/github.com/istio/istio)\n5: [![GoDoc](https://godoc.org/istio.io/istio?status.svg)](https://godoc.org/istio.io/istio)\n6: \n7: <a href=\"https://istio.io/\">\n8:     <picture>\n9:       <source media=\"(prefers-color-scheme: dark)\" srcset=\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cncf/artwork/refs/heads/main/projects/istio/icon/color/istio-icon-color.svg\">\n10:       <source media=\"(prefers-color-scheme: light)\" srcset=\"https://github.com/istio/istio/raw/master/logo/istio-bluelogo-whitebackground-unframed.svg\">\n11:       <img title=\"Istio\" height=\"100\" width=\"100\" alt=\"Istio logo\" src=\"https://github.com/istio/istio/raw/master/logo/istio-bluelogo-whitebackground-unframed.svg\">\n12:     </picture>\n13: </a>\n14: \n15: ---\n16: \n17: Istio is an open source service mesh that layers transparently onto existing distributed applications. Istio\u2019s powerful features provide a uniform and more efficient way to secure, connect, and monitor services. Istio is the path to load balancing, service-to-service authentication, and monitoring \u2013 with few or no service code changes.\n18: \n19: - For in-depth information about how to use Istio, visit [istio.io](https://istio.io)\n20: - To ask questions and get assistance from our community, visit [GitHub Discussions](https://github.com/istio/istio/discussions)\n21: - To learn how to participate in our overall community, visit [our community page](https://istio.io/about/community)\n22: \n23: In this README:\n24: \n25: - [Introduction](#introduction)\n26: - [Repositories](#repositories)\n27: - [Issue management](#issue-management)\n28: \n29: In addition, here are some other documents you may wish to read:\n30: \n31: - [Istio Community](https://github.com/istio/community#istio-community) - describes how to get involved and contribute to the Istio project\n32: - [Istio Developer's Guide](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Preparing-for-Development) - explains how to set up and use an Istio development environment\n33: - [Project Conventions](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Development-Conventions) - describes the conventions we use within the code base\n34: - [Creating Fast and Lean Code](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Writing-Fast-and-Lean-Code) - performance-oriented advice and guidelines for the code base\n35: \n36: You'll find many other useful documents on our [Wiki](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki).\n37: \n38: ## Introduction\n39: \n40: [Istio](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/what-is-istio/) is an open platform for providing a uniform way to [integrate\n41: microservices](https://istio.io/latest/docs/examples/microservices-istio/), manage [traffic flow](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/traffic-management/) across microservices, enforce policies\n42: and aggregate telemetry data. Istio's control plane provides an abstraction\n43: layer over the underlying cluster management platform, such as Kubernetes.\n44: \n45: Istio is composed of these components:\n46: \n47: - **Envoy** - Sidecar proxies per microservice to handle ingress/egress traffic\n48:    between services in the cluster and from a service to external\n49:    services. The proxies form a _secure microservice mesh_ providing a rich\n50:    set of functions like discovery, rich layer-7 routing, circuit breakers,\n51:    policy enforcement and telemetry recording/reporting\n52:    functions.\n53: \n54:   > Note: The service mesh is not an overlay network. It\n55:   > simplifies and enhances how microservices in an application talk to each\n56:   > other over the network provided by the underlying platform.\n57: \n58: * **Ztunnel** - A lightweight data plane proxy written in Rust,\n59:     used in Ambient mesh mode to provide secure connectivity and observability for workloads without sidecar proxies.\n60: \n61: - **Istiod** - The Istio control plane. It provides service discovery, configuration and certificate management.\n62: \n63: ## Repositories\n64: \n65: The Istio project is divided across a few GitHub repositories:\n66: \n67: - [istio/api](https://github.com/istio/api). This repository defines\n68: component-level APIs and common configuration formats for the Istio platform.\n69: \n70: - [istio/community](https://github.com/istio/community). This repository contains\n71: information on the Istio community, including the various documents that govern\n72: the Istio open source project.\n73: \n74: - [istio/istio](README.md). This is the main code repository. It hosts Istio's\n75: core components, install artifacts, and sample programs. It includes:\n76: \n77:     - [istioctl](istioctl/). This directory contains code for the\n78: [_istioctl_](https://istio.io/latest/docs/reference/commands/istioctl/) command line utility.\n79: \n80:     - [pilot](pilot/). This directory\n81: contains platform-specific code to populate the\n82: [abstract service model](https://istio.io/docs/concepts/traffic-management/#pilot), dynamically reconfigure the proxies\n83: when the application topology changes, as well as translate\n84: [routing rules](https://istio.io/latest/docs/reference/config/networking/) into proxy specific configuration.\n85: \n86:     - [security](security/). This directory contains [security](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/security/) related code.\n87: \n88: - [istio/proxy](https://github.com/istio/proxy). The Istio proxy contains\n89: extensions to the [Envoy proxy](https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy) (in the form of\n90: Envoy filters) that support authentication, authorization, and telemetry collection.\n91: \n92: - [istio/ztunnel](https://github.com/istio/ztunnel). The repository contains the Rust implementation of the ztunnel\n93: component of Ambient mesh.\n94: \n95: - [istio/client-go](https://github.com/istio/client-go). This repository defines\n96:   auto-generated Kubernetes clients for interacting with Istio resources programmatically.\n97: \n98: > [!NOTE]\n99: > Only the `istio/api` and `istio/client-go` repositories expose stable interfaces intended for direct usage as libraries.\n100: \n101: ## Issue management\n102: \n103: We use GitHub to track all of our bugs and feature requests. Each issue we track has a variety of metadata:\n104: \n105: - **Epic**. An epic represents a feature area for Istio as a whole. Epics are fairly broad in scope and are basically product-level things.\n106: Each issue is ultimately part of an epic.\n107: \n108: - **Milestone**. Each issue is assigned a milestone. This is 0.1, 0.2, ..., or 'Nebulous Future'. The milestone indicates when we\n109: think the issue should get addressed.\n110: \n111: - **Priority**.   "content": "# Istio Control Plane Developer Onboarding Guide\n\nWelcome to Istio! This guide will help you understand the control plane architecture, set up your development environment, and make your first contribution.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Build Prerequisites](#build-prerequisites)\n2. [Architecture Overview](#architecture-overview)\n3. [First Contribution Workflow](#first-contribution-workflow)\n4. [Debugging and Development](#debugging-and-development)\n5. [Key Resources](#key-resources)\n\n---\n\n## Build Prerequisites\n\n### System Requirements\n\n**Go Version**: 1.25.0 or later (as specified in `go.mod`)\n\nVerify your Go installation:\n```bash\ngo version\n```\n\n### Environment Setup\n\n**Clone the Repository** (with all submodules):\n```bash\ngit clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/istio/istio.git\ncd istio\n```\n\nIf you've already cloned without submodules, initialize them:\n```bash\ngit submodule update --init --recursive\n```\n\n### Build System\n\nIstio uses a Makefile-based build system with two modes:\n\n#### Option 1: Local Build (Recommended for Development)\n\n```bash\nmake build\n```\n\nThis compiles binaries directly on your machine. You'll need:\n- Go toolchain\n- Standard build tools (gcc, make)\n\n#### Option 2: Containerized Build\n\nFor a completely isolated environment (fewer system dependencies):\n```bash\nBUILD_WITH_CONTAINER=1 make build\n```\n\nThis uses Docker to build everything in a consistent container environment. Requires Docker to be installed.\n\n### Core Binaries\n\nThe main control plane binaries built by the system are:\n\n- **`pilot-discovery`**: The core Istio discovery server, handles xDS protocol and configuration distribution\n  - Location: `./pilot/cmd/pilot-discovery`\n  - Built target: `$GOBIN/pilot-discovery`\n\n- **`pilot-agent`**: Sidecar agent that runs in each Envoy pod, manages local configuration\n  - Location: `./pilot/cmd/pilot-agent`\n  - Built target: `$GOBIN/pilot-agent`\n\n- **`istioctl`**: CLI tool for debugging and managing Istio\n  - Location: `./istioctl/cmd/istioctl`\n  - Built target: `$GOBIN/istioctl`\n\nTo build individual binaries:\n```bash\nmake pilot-discovery\nmake pilot-agent\nmake istioctl\n```\n\n### Running Tests\n\n**Unit Tests with Race Detection** (recommended):\n```bash\nmake test\n```\n\nThis runs: `go test ./... -race -tags=assert`\n\n**Run Tests for Specific Packages**:\n```bash\n# Test only the pilot package\nPKG=./pilot/... make test\n\n# Test only xDS discovery server\nPKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/... make test\n```\n\n**Run Benchmarks**:\n```bash\nmake benchtest\n```\n\n### Pre-commit Checks\n\nBefore submitting a PR, run the complete pre-commit pipeline:\n```bash\nmake precommit\n```\n\nThis runs:\n- `make fmt` - Code formatting (gofmt, goimports)\n- `make lint` - Linting (go vet, copyright banners, scripts, YAML, markdown, etc.)\n- `make tidy-go` - Dependency management\n\n**Just formatting**:\n```bash\nmake format\n```\n\n---\n\n## Architecture Overview\n\n### Control Plane Components\n\nIstio's control plane (istiod) is a single unified binary that merges three historical components:\n\n1. **Pilot** - Service discovery and traffic management\n   - Watches Kubernetes Services and ServiceEntry resources\n   - Generates xDS configuration for Envoy proxies\n   - Implements traffic policies (routing, load balancing, retries)\n\n2. **Citadel** - Certificate Authority and Identity Management\n   - Issues and manages mTLS certificates for workloads\n   - Provides certificate rotation and distribution\n   - Manages certificate revocation\n\n3. **Galley** - Configuration validation and distribution\n   - Validates Istio CRDs and Kubernetes resources\n   - Distributes validated configurations to other components\n\n### xDS Protocol: Configuration Distribution\n\nThe **xDS API** is the core protocol by which istiod pushes configuration to Envoy proxies. It consists of four main resource types:\n\n- **CDS** (Cluster Discovery Service): Defines upstream services as \"clusters\"\n  - Each cluster represents a service that traffic can be sent to\n  - Includes load balancing policies and health checks\n  - Generated by: `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go`\n\n- **EDS** (Endpoint Discovery Service): Lists IP addresses for each cluster\n  - Provides the actual endpoints (pods) behind each service\n  - Updated when pods start/stop or change state\n  - Generated by: `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go`\n\n- **LDS** (Listener Discovery Service): Defines listening sockets on the proxy\n  - Specifies ports and protocols the Envoy proxy should listen on\n  - Configures filter chains for different traffic types\n  - Generated by: `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go`\n\n- **RDS** (Route Discovery Service): Defines routing rules\n  - Specifies how to route traffic between services\n  - Implements VirtualService, DestinationRule, and traffic policies\n  - Generated by: `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go`\n\n### Data Flow: Service Discovery to xDS Push\n\nHere's the complete end-to-end flow when a new service is discovered:\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 1. CONFIGURATION GENERATION                                     \u2502\n\u2502    For each connected proxy, generators build xDS resources:   \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    CDS Generator (xds/cds.go)                                  \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Calls ConfigGenerator.BuildClusters()                     \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Creates Cluster resources for all services                \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    EDS Generator (xds/eds.go)                                  \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Calls ConfigGenerator.BuildEndpoints()                    \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Creates ClusterLoadAssignment for each cluster            \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Reads from EndpointIndex (service discovery)              \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    LDS Generator (xds/lds.go)                                  \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Calls ConfigGenerator.BuildListeners()                    \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Creates Listener resources on proxy's ports               \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    RDS Generator (xds/rds.go)                                  \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Calls ConfigGenerator.BuildRoutes()                       \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Creates RouteConfiguration with VirtualService rules     \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    Key files:                                                  \u2502\n\u2502    - pilot/pkg/networking/core/configgen.go (ConfigGenerator) \u2502\n\u2502    - pilot/pkg/xds/v3/ (xDS generators)                       \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                     \u2502\n                     \u25bc\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 6. XDS PUSH TO PROXIES                                          \u2502\n\u2502    DiscoveryServer.AdsPushAll() or AdsPush()                   \u2502\n\u2502    sends update via gRPC to all connected Envoy proxies        \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    Protocols:                                                  \u2502\n\u2502    - ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service): Single gRPC stream    \u2502\n\u2502    - Delta xDS: Incremental updates                            \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    Key files:                                                  \u2502\n\u2502    - xds/ads.go (ADS protocol)                                 \u2502\n\u2502    - xds/delta.go (Delta xDS)                                  \u2502\n\u2502    - xds/discovery.go (Push implementation)                    \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                     \u2502\n                     \u25bc\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 7. xDS Protocol Implementation\n- **discovery.go**: Core DiscoveryServer that manages gRPC connections and pushes\n- **ads.go**: ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) protocol handler\n- **delta.go**: Delta xDS incremental update handler\n- **cds.go, eds.go, lds.go, rds.go**: Individual xDS resource generators\n- **monitoring.go**: Metrics for push operations and timing\n\n**Entry point**: `DiscoveryServer` struct in discovery.go:64\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` - Service Discovery\nMultiple registry implementations:\n- **kube/controller/**: Kubernetes service discovery (watches K8s API)\n- **serviceentry/**: ServiceEntry resource discovery\n- **aggregate/**: Combines multiple registries\n\n**Key interface**: `Instance` interface for service registries\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/bootstrap/` - Server Initialization\n- **server.go**: Main Server struct (line 105) that orchestrates istiod startup\n- **servicecontroller.go**: Initializes all service registries\n- **configcontroller.go**: Sets up configuration watchers for CRDs\n- **discovery.go**: Initializes xDS generators\n- **istio_ca.go**: Certificate Authority initialization\n- **mesh.go**: Mesh configuration loading\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/model/` - Core Data Models\n- **environment.go**: Global Environment with ServiceDiscovery, ConfigStore\n- **push.go**: PushContext and PushRequest (configuration version)\n- **proxy.go**: Proxy model representing an Envoy instance\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/networking/` - Configuration Generation\n- **core/configgen.go**: ConfigGenerator interface for building xDS resources\n- **core/v1alpha3/**: Legacy traffic management implementation\n- **security/authz/**: Authorization policy generation\n- **policy/**: Traffic policy implementation\n\n#### `security/pkg/` - Certificate Management\n- **pki/**: Private key infrastructure and CA operations\n- **server/ca/**: CA server for certificate issuance\n- **credentials/**: Certificate distribution and management\n\n### Service Registry Integration with Kubernetes\n\nThe service registry is the bridge between Kubernetes state and Istio configuration:\n\n1. **Kubernetes Controller** (serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go)\n   - Watches Kubernetes Service, Endpoints, and Pod objects\n   - Normalizes K8s concepts into Istio's abstract Service model\n   - Triggers push events when services or endpoints change\n\n2. **Service Model** (model/service.go)\n   - Abstract representation of a service (hostname, ports, endpoints)\n   - Platform-independent - works with K8s, ServiceEntry, etc.\n\n3. **Configuration Updates**\n   - When a Service or Endpoint changes, the registry notifies\n   - This triggers a PushRequest with reason `ServiceUpdate`\n   - The configuration generators use the updated registry to build new xDS resources\n\n**Example**: When you deploy a new pod in Kubernetes:\n- API server creates an Endpoint object\n- Controller watches Endpoints API\n- Controller triggers `ServiceUpdate` PushRequest\n- EDS generator reads updated endpoints\n- xDS push sent to all proxies with new endpoints\n\n---\n\n## First Contribution Workflow\n\n### Finding a Good First Issue\n\n1. Visit the [Istio GitHub Issues page](https://github.com/istio/istio/issues)\n2. Filter by label `kind/feature` or `kind/bug`\n3. Look for issues with `good-first-issue` label\n4. Priority levels: P0 (critical), P1 (important), P2 (nice-to-have)\n\n### Setting Up Your Fork\n\n```bash\n# Fork the repository on GitHub (click Fork button)\n\n# Clone your fork\ngit clone https://github.com/YOUR_USERNAME/istio.git\ncd istio\n\n# Add upstream remote for syncing\ngit remote add upstream https://github.com/istio/istio.git\n\n# Create a feature branch\ngit checkout -b my-feature-branch\n```\n\n### Making Code Changes\n\n#### Understanding the Code\n\nBefore making changes, understand the call path:\n1. Identify which component(s) your change affects (Pilot, Citadel, networking, etc.)\n2. Locate the relevant source files in that component\n3. Use `grep` or IDE search to find all callers/usages\n4. Read the tests to understand expected behavior\n\n#### Writing Your Change\n\n1. Make minimal, focused changes to address the issue\n2. Don't refactor surrounding code unless necessary\n3. Add comments only for non-obvious logic\n4. Follow existing code style in the file\n\n#### Running Tests Locally\n\n**For the files you changed**:\n```bash\n# Find all affected packages\n# Example: if you edited pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go\nPKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/... make test\n\n# Or be more specific\ngo test ./pilot/pkg/xds -v -race\n```\n\n**Write unit tests for new functionality**:\n```go\n// In discovery_test.go\nfunc TestMyNewFeature(t *testing.T) {\n    // Setup\n    // Act\n    // Assert\n}\n```\n\n**Run pre-commit checks** (required before submitting):\n```bash\nmake precommit\n```\n\nThis will:\n- Auto-format code with `gofmt` and `goimports`\n- Run linters (go vet, copyright headers, shell scripts, etc.)\n- Check for common mistakes\n\n### Creating a Pull Request\n\n1. **Commit your changes**:\n```bash\ngit add .\ngit commit -m \"Brief description of change\n\nLonger explanation if needed. Reference issue: #12345\"\n```\n\n2. **Push to your fork**:\n```bash\ngit push origin my-feature-branch\n```\n\n3. **Create PR on GitHub**:\n   - Title: Be concise and descriptive\n   - Description: Explain what and why (the how is in the code)\n   - Link issue: \"Fixes #12345\" or \"Related to #12345\"\n\n4. **PR Requirements and CI Gates**:\n   - [ ] All tests pass (automated via GitHub Actions)\n   - [ ] At least 2 approvals from maintainers\n   - [ ] Code review comments addressed\n   - [ ] No merge conflicts with main branch\n   - [ ] Signed CLA (Contributor License Agreement)\n\n5. **Common Reviewer Feedback**:\n   - Add/improve unit tests\n   - Simplify code or add explanatory comments\n   - Consider edge cases\n   - Match existing patterns in the codebase\n\n### PR Review Checklist\n\nBefore submitting, make sure:\n\n- [ ] `make precommit` passes without errors\n- [ ] `make test PKG=<modified-package>/... ` passes\n- [ ] No TODO comments or debug code\n- [ ] Commit message is clear and references the issue\n- [ ] Changes are minimal and focused on the issue\n- [ ] Backwards compatible (unless breaking change approved)\n\n---\n\n## Debugging and Development\n\n### Useful Make Targets\n\n```bash\n# Build without testing\nmake build\n\n# Build for Linux (for container images)\nmake build-linux\n\n# Run all tests with race features\n\n# Build output\nTARGET_OUT=./out/linux          # Where binaries are placed\n\n# Istio config\nISTIO_NAMESPACE=istio-system\n```\n\n### Using the Test Utilities\n\nThe codebase includes excellent test utilities:\n\n**pilot/test/xds/fake.go**:\n- FakeDiscoveryServer: Mock xDS server for testing\n- Helps test proxy configuration without running full istiod\n\n**pilot/test/xdstest/extract.go**:\n- Extract listeners, clusters, routes from xDS resources\n- Validate xDS response structure\n\n**Example test**:\n```go\nimport \"istio.io/istio/pilot/test/xds\"\n\nfunc TestMyChange(t *testing.T) {\n    ds := xds.NewFakeDiscoveryServer(t, xds.FakeOptions{})\n    defer ds.Cleanup()\n\n    // Test configuration generation\n    proxy := &model.Proxy{ID: \"pod.namespace\"}\n    clusters := ds.Clusters(proxy)\n\n    // Assert clusters are correct\n    if len(clusters) == 0 {\n        t.Fatal(\"Expected clusters\")\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Key Resources\n\n### Official Documentation\n- [Istio Architecture](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/what-is-istio/)\n- [Istio Developer's This guide will help you understand the control plane architecture, set up your development environment, and make your first contribution.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Build Prerequisites](#build-prerequisites)\n2. [Architecture Overview](#architecture-overview)\n3. [First Contribution Workflow](#first-contribution-workflow)\n4. [Debugging and Development](#debugging-and-development)\n5. [Key Resources](#key-resources)\n\n---\n\n## Build Prerequisites\n\n### System Requirements\n\n**Go Version**: 1.25.0 or later (as specified in `go.mod`)\n\nVerify your Go installation:\n```bash\ngo version\n```\n\n### Environment Setup\n\n**Clone the Repository** (with all submodules):\n```bash\ngit clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/istio/istio.git\ncd istio\n```\n\nIf you've already cloned without submodules, initialize them:\n```bash\ngit submodule update --init --recursive\n```\n\n### Build System\n\nIstio uses a Makefile-based build system with two modes:\n\n#### Option 1: Local Build (Recommended for Development)\n\n```bash\nmake build\n```\n\nThis compiles binaries directly on your machine. You'll need:\n- Go toolchain\n- Standard build tools (gcc, make)\n\n#### Option 2: Containerized Build\n\nFor a completely isolated environment (fewer system dependencies):\n```bash\nBUILD_WITH_CONTAINER=1 make build\n```\n\nThis uses Docker to build everything in a consistent container environment. Requires Docker to be installed.\n\n### Core Binaries\n\nThe main control plane binaries built by the system are:\n\n- **`pilot-discovery`**: The core Istio discovery server, handles xDS protocol and configuration distribution\n  - Location: `./pilot/cmd/pilot-discovery`\n  - Built target: `$GOBIN/pilot-discovery`\n\n- **`pilot-agent`**: Sidecar agent that runs in each Envoy pod, manages local configuration\n  - Location: `./pilot/cmd/pilot-agent`\n  - Built target: `$GOBIN/pilot-agent`\n\n- **`istioctl`**: CLI tool for debugging and managing Istio\n  - Location: `./istioctl/cmd/istioctl`\n  - Built target: `$GOBIN/istioctl`\n\nTo build individual binaries:\n```bash\nmake pilot-discovery\nmake pilot-agent\nmake istioctl\n```\n\n### Running Tests\n\n**Unit Tests with Race Detection** (recommended):\n```bash\nmake test\n```\n\nThis runs: `go test ./... -race -tags=assert`\n\n**Run Tests for Specific Packages**:\n```bash\n# Test only the pilot package\nPKG=./pilot/... make test\n\n# Test only xDS discovery server\nPKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/... make test\n```\n\n**Run Benchmarks**:\n```bash\nmake benchtest\n```\n\n### Pre-commit Checks\n\nBefore submitting a PR, run the complete pre-commit pipeline:\n```bash\nmake precommit\n```\n\nThis runs:\n- `make fmt` - Code formatting (gofmt, goimports)\n- `make lint` - Linting (go vet, copyright banners, scripts, YAML, markdown, etc.)\n- `make tidy-go` - Dependency management\n\n**Just formatting**:\n```bash\nmake format\n```\n\n---\n\n## Architecture Overview\n\n### Control Plane Components\n\nIstio's control plane (istiod) is a single unified binary that merges three historical components:\n\n1. **Pilot** - Service discovery and traffic management\n   - Watches Kubernetes Services and ServiceEntry resources\n   - Generates xDS configuration for Envoy proxies\n   - Implements traffic policies (routing, load balancing, retries)\n\n2. **Citadel** - Certificate Authority and Identity Management\n   - Issues and manages mTLS certificates for workloads\n   - Provides certificate rotation and distribution\n   - Manages certificate revocation\n\n3. **Galley** - Configuration validation and distribution\n   - Validates Istio CRDs and Kubernetes resources\n   - Distributes validated configurations to other components\n\n### xDS Protocol: Configuration Distribution\n\nThe **xDS API** is the core protocol by which istiod pushes configuration to Envoy proxies. It consists of four main resource types:\n\n- **CDS** (Cluster Discovery Service): Defines upstream services as \"clusters\"\n  - Each cluster represents a service that traffic can be sent to\n  - Includes load balancing policies and health checks\n  - Generated by: `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go`\n\n- **EDS** (Endpoint Discovery Service): Lists IP addresses for each cluster\n  - Provides the actual endpoints (pods) behind each service\n  - Updated when pods start/stop or change state\n  - Generated by: `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go`\n\n- **LDS** (Listener Discovery Service): Defines listening sockets on the proxy\n  - Specifies ports and protocols the Envoy proxy should listen on\n  - Configures filter chains for different traffic types\n  - Generated by: `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go`\n\n- **RDS** (Route Discovery Service): Defines routing rules\n  - Specifies how to route traffic between services\n  - Implements VirtualService, DestinationRule, and traffic policies\n  - Generated by: `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go`\n\n### Data Flow: Service Discovery to xDS Push\n\nHere's the complete end-to-end flow when a new service is discovered:\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 1. SERVICE REGISTRATION                                         \u2502\n\u2502    Kubernetes API Server creates a Service object               \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                     \u2502\n                     \u25bc\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 2. SERVICE DISCOVERY                                            \u2502\n\u2502    ServiceRegistry (pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/)                \u2502\n\u2502    - KubeRegistry watches Kubernetes Services                  \u2502\n\u2502    - ServiceEntryRegistry watches ServiceEntry CRDs            \u2502\n\u2502    - AggregateRegistry combines multiple registries            \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    Key files:                                                  \u2502\n\u2502    - serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go              \u2502\n\u2502    - serviceregistry/serviceentry/controller.go                \u2502\n\u2502    - serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go                   \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                     \u2502\n                     \u25bc\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 3. CONFIGURATION UPDATE TRIGGER                                 \u2502\n\u2502    ServiceDiscovery emits event \u2192 PushRequest created           \u2502\n\u2502    Request queued in DiscoveryServer.pushChannel               \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    Key files:                                                  \u2502\n\u2502    - xds/discovery.go (DiscoveryServer.push handler)           \u2502\n\u2502    - model/push.go (PushRequest/PushContext)                   \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                     \u2502\n                     \u25bc\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 4. DEBOUNCING & CONTEXT INITIALIZATION                         \u2502\n\u2502    Multiple events batched for efficiency                       \u2502\n\u2502    initPushContext() builds new model.PushContext with:        \u2502\n\u2502    - Current service registry state                            \u2502\n\u2502    - Mesh configuration                                        \u2502\n\u2502    - All defined VirtualServices and DestinationRules         \u2502\n\u2502    - Security policies                                         \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    Key files:                                                  \u2502\n\u2502    - model/pushcontext.go (PushContext initialization)         \u2502\n\u2502    - xds/discovery.go:initPushContext()                       \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                     \u2502\n                     \u25bc\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 5. pilot/pkg/networking/core/configgen.go (ConfigGenerator) \u2502\n\u2502    - pilot/pkg/xds/v3/ (xDS generators)                       \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                     \u2502\n                     \u25bc\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 6. XDS PUSH TO PROXIES                                          \u2502\n\u2502    DiscoveryServer.AdsPushAll() or AdsPush()                   \u2502\n\u2502    sends update via gRPC to all connected Envoy proxies        \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    Protocols:                                                  \u2502\n\u2502    - ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service): Single gRPC stream    \u2502\n\u2502    - Delta xDS: Incremental updates                            \u2502\n\u2502                                                                 \u2502\n\u2502    Key files:                                                  \u2502\n\u2502    - xds/ads.go (ADS protocol)                                 \u2502\n\u2502    - xds/delta.go (Delta xDS)                                  \u2502\n\u2502    - xds/discovery.go (Push implementation)                    \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                     \u2502\n                     \u25bc\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 7. PROXY APPLICATION                                            \u2502\n\u2502    Envoy proxy receives xDS update                             \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Updates local routing configuration                       \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Applies new clusters, endpoints, listeners, routes        \u2502\n\u2502    \u2192 Traffic now flows according to new configuration          \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n```\n\n### Key Packages and Their Responsibilities\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/xds/` - xDS Protocol Implementation\n- **discovery.go**: Core DiscoveryServer that manages gRPC connections and pushes\n- **ads.go**: ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) protocol handler\n- **delta.go**: Delta xDS incremental update handler\n- **cds.go, eds.go, lds.go, rds.go**: Individual xDS resource generators\n- **monitoring.go**: Metrics for push operations and timing\n\n**Entry point**: `DiscoveryServer` struct in discovery.go:64\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` - Service Discovery\nMultiple registry implementations:\n- **kube/controller/**: Kubernetes service discovery (watches K8s API)\n- **serviceentry/**: ServiceEntry resource discovery\n- **aggregate/**: Combines multiple registries\n\n**Key interface**: `Instance` interface for service registries\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/bootstrap/` - Server Initialization\n- **server.go**: Main Server struct (line 105) that orchestrates istiod startup\n- **servicecontroller.go**: Initializes all service registries\n- **configcontroller.go**: Sets up configuration watchers for CRDs\n- **discovery.go**: Initializes xDS generators\n- **istio_ca.go**: Certificate Authority initialization\n- **mesh.go**: Mesh configuration loading\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/model/` - Core Data Models\n- **environment.go**: Global Environment with ServiceDiscovery, ConfigStore\n- **push.go**: PushContext and PushRequest (configuration version)\n- **proxy.go**: Proxy model representing an Envoy instance\n\n#### `pilot/pkg/networking/` - Configuration Generation\n- **core/configgen.go**: ConfigGenerator interface for building xDS resources\n- **core/v1alpha3/**: Legacy traffic management implementation\n- **security/authz/**: Authorization policy generation\n- **policy/**: Traffic policy implementation\n\n#### `security/pkg/` - Certificate Management\n- **pki/**: Private key infrastructure and CA operations\n- **server/ca/**: CA server for certificate issuance\n- **credentials/**: Certificate distribution and management\n\n### Service Registry Integration with Kubernetes\n\nThe service registry is the bridge between Kubernetes state and Istio configuration:\n\n1. **Kubernetes Controller** (serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go)\n   - Watches Kubernetes Service, Endpoints, and Pod objects\n   - Normalizes K8s concepts into Istio's abstract Service model\n   - Triggers push events when services or endpoints change\n\n2. **Service Model** (model/service.go)\n   - Abstract representation of a service (hostname, ports, endpoints)\n   - Platform-independent - works with K8s, ServiceEntry, etc.\n\n3. **Configuration Updates**\n   - When a Service or Endpoint changes, the registry notifies\n   - This triggers a PushRequest with reason `ServiceUpdate`\n   - The configuration generators use the updated registry to build new xDS resources\n\n**Example**: When you deploy a new pod in Kubernetes:\n- API server creates an Endpoint object\n- Controller watches Endpoints API\n- Controller triggers `ServiceUpdate` PushRequest\n- EDS generator reads updated endpoints\n- xDS push sent to all proxies with new endpoints\n\n---\n\n## First Contribution Workflow\n\n### Finding a Good First Issue\n\n1. Visit the [Istio GitHub Issues page](https://github.com/istio/istio/issues)\n2. Filter by label `kind/feature` or `kind/bug`\n3. Look for issues with `good-first-issue` label\n4. Priority levels: P0 (critical), P1 (important), P2 (nice-to-have)\n\n### Setting Up Your Fork\n\n```bash\n# Fork the repository on GitHub (click Fork button)\n\n# Clone your fork\ngit clone https://github.com/YOUR_USERNAME/istio.git\ncd istio\n\n# Add upstream remote for syncing\ngit remote add upstream https://github.com/istio/istio.git\n\n# Create a feature branch\ngit checkout -b my-feature-branch\n```\n\n### Making Code Changes\n\n#### Understanding the Code\n\nBefore making changes, understand the call path:\n1. Identify which component(s) your change affects (Pilot, Citadel, networking, etc.)\n2. Locate the relevant source files in that component\n3. Use `grep` or IDE search to find all callers/usages\n4. Read the tests to understand expected behavior\n\n#### Writing Your Change\n\n1. Make minimal, focused changes to address the issue\n2. Don't refactor surrounding code unless necessary\n3. Add comments only for non-obvious logic\n4. Follow existing code style in the file\n\n#### Running Tests Locally\n\n**For the files you changed**:\n```bash\n# Find all affected packages\n# Example: if you edited pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go\nPKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/... make test\n\n# Or be more specific\ngo test ./pilot/pkg/xds -v -race\n```\n\n**Write unit tests for new functionality**:\n```go\n// In discovery_test.go\nfunc TestMyNewFeature(t *testing.T) {\n    // Setup\n    // Act\n    // Assert\n}\n```\n\n**Run pre-commit checks** (required before submitting):\n```bash\nmake precommit\n```\n\nThis will:\n- Auto-format code with `gofmt` and `goimports`\n- Run linters (go vet, copyright headers, shell scripts, etc.)\n- Check for common mistakes\n\n### Creating a Pull Request\n\n1. **Commit your changes**:\n```bash\ngit add .\ngit commit -m \"Brief description of change\n\nLonger explanation if needed. Reference issue: #12345\"\n```\n\n2. **Push to your fork**:\n```bash\ngit push origin my-feature-branch\n```\n\n3. **Create PR on GitHub**:\n   - Title: Be concise and descriptive\n   - Description: Explain what and why (the how is in the code)\n   - Link issue: \"Fixes #12345\" or \"Related to #12345\"\n\n4. **PR Requirements and CI Gates**:\n   - [ ] All tests pass (automated via GitHub Actions)\n   - [ ] At least 2 approvals from maintainers\n   - [ ] Code review comments addressed\n   - [ ] No merge conflicts with main branch\n   - [ ] Signed CLA (Contributor License Agreement)\n\n5. **Common Reviewer Feedback**:\n   - Add/improve unit tests\n   - Simplify code or add explanatory comments\n   - Consider edge cases\n   - Match existing patterns in the codebase\n\n### PR Review Checklist\n\nBefore submitting, make sure:\n\n- [ ] `make precommit` passes without errors\n- [ ] `make test PKG=<modified-package>/... ` passes\n- [ ] No TODO comments or debug code\n- [ ] Commit message is clear and references the issue\n- [ ] Changes are minimal and focused on the issue\n- [ ] Backwards compatible (unless breaking change approved)\n\n---\n\n## Debugging and Development\n\n### Useful Make Targets\n\n```bash\n# Build without testing\nmake build\n\n# Build for Linux (for container images)\nmake build-linux\n\n# Run all tests with race detection\nmake test\n\n# Run tests for specific package\nPKG=./pilot/pkg/xds/... make test\n\n# Format code\nmake format\n\n# Run linters\nmake lint\n\n# Full pre-commit pipeline\nmake precommit\n\n# Show available targets\nmake help\n```\n\n### Debugging istiod Locally\n\n**Run istiod with debug logging**:\n```bash\nDEBUG=1 make build\n```\n\n**Access debug endpoints** (when istiod is running):\n```bash\n# View current mesh configuration\ncurl http://localhost:8080/debug/mesh\n\n# View connected proxies\ncurl http://localhost:8080/debug/connections\n\n# View current push context\ncurl http://localhost:8080/debug/pushcontext\n\n# View config for a specific proxy\ncurl http://localhost:8080/debug/config_dump?proxyID=<pod-name>.<namespace>\n```\n\n### Environment Variables for Development\n\nKey environment variables you might use:\n\n```bash\n# Go build tags\nAGENT_TAGS=agent,disable_pgv    # For lightweight agents\nSTANDARD_TAGS=vtprotobuf        # For full features\n\n# Build output\nTARGET_OUT=./out/linux          # Where binaries are placed\n\n# Istio config\nISTIO_NAMESPACE=istio-system\n```\n\n### Using the Test Utilities\n\nThe codebase includes excellent test utilities:\n\n**pilot/test/xds/fake.go**:\n- FakeDiscoveryServer: Mock xDS server for testing\n- Helps test proxy configuration without running full istiod\n\n**pilot/test/xdstest/extract.go**:\n- Extract listeners, clusters, routes from xDS resources\n- Validate xDS response structure\n\n**Example test**:\n```go\nimport \"istio.io/istio/pilot/test/xds\"\n\nfunc TestMyChange(t *testing.T) {\n    ds := xds.NewFakeDiscoveryServer(t, xds.FakeOptions{})\n    defer ds.Cleanup()\n\n    // Test configuration generation\n    proxy := &model.Proxy{ID: \"pod.namespace\"}\n    clusters := ds.Clusters(proxy)\n\n    // Assert clusters are correct\n    if len(clusters) == 0 {\n        t.Fatal(\"Expected clusters\")\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Key Resources\n\n### Official Documentation\n- [Istio Architecture](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/what-is-istio/)\n- [Istio Developer's Guide](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Preparing-for-Development)\n- [Development Conventions](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Development-Conventions)\n\n### Code Navigation Tips\n\n**Finding the code for a feature**:\n1. User-facing config? Check `pilot/pkg/networking/core/v1alpha3/`\n2. Service discovery? Check `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/`\n3. Certificate management? Check `security/pkg/`\n4. Metrics/observability? Check `pilot/pkg/xds/monitoring.go`\n\n**Understanding xDS generation**:\n1. Start at `pilot/pkg/bootstrap/discovery.go:InitGenerators()`\n2. All the code flows through this pipeline.\n\nGood luck with your first contribution!\n",

# Istio Control Plane Developer Onboarding Guide

Welcome to Istio! This guide will help you understand the control plane architecture, set up your development environment, and make your first contribution.

## Table of Contents

1. [Build Prerequisites](#build-prerequisites)
2. [Architecture Overview](#architecture-overview)
3. [First Contribution Workflow](#first-contribution-workflow)
4. [Debugging and Development](#debugging-and-development)
5. [Key Resources](#key-resources)

---

## Build Prerequisites

### System Requirements

**Go Version**: 1.25.0 or later (as specified in `go.mod`)

Verify your Go installation:
```bash
go version
```

### Environment Setup

**Clone the Repository** (with all submodules):
```bash
git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/istio/istio.git
cd istio
```

If you've already cloned without submodules, initialize them:
```bash
git submodule update --init --recursive
```

### Build System

Istio uses a Makefile-based build system with two modes:

#### Option 1: Local Build (Recommended for Development)

```bash
make build
```

This compiles binaries directly on your machine. You'll need:
- Go toolchain
- Standard build tools (gcc, make)

#### Option 2: Containerized Build

For a completely isolated environment (fewer system dependencies):
```bash
BUILD_WITH_CONTAINER=1 make build
```

This uses Docker to build everything in a consistent container environment. Requires Docker to be installed.

### Core Binaries

The main control plane binaries built by the system are:

- **`pilot-discovery`**: The core Istio discovery server, handles xDS protocol and configuration distribution
  - Location: `./pilot/cmd/pilot-discovery`
  - Built target: `$GOBIN/pilot-discovery`
